Aziza ¬†Aziza is a Lebanese singer and song writer whose musical world combines classical Arabic Tarab rules of composition, with Pop music. Her father was a singer in the 70‚Äôs and 80‚Äôs. Tarapop is a mix of sounds inspired from the region, such as Chaabi Egyptian, Lebanese and literary Arabic. This fusion is what leads to a musical version proper to Beirut today: an eclectic, electric, story-driven palette of styles. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In that sense, Aziza's original music tells the story of the age she lives in, and the constant necessity of grounding herself in a turmoiled environment. Tarapop is classical vocals, rhythms and arrangement (ground) interpreted live with a backing pop rock band, taking the sounds of the quarter notes to new dynamics. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Aziza's self titled all originals debut album was released in 2014. &nbsp;Ya Salat El Zein a classical egyptian cover song was revisited by Aziza and Michel Fadel in 2016 . 3alamna Wahed ‚ÄúOur World is One‚Äù a song written by Aziza for the World Cup 2018 with a message that reunites the arabic world with all its differences , produced and available on Anghami. &nbsp;Get the A2 limited (5 remaining shirts) at <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/redirect?event=video_description&amp;redir_token=QUFFLUhqazMyTEtRaXMtTDEtR2o0OHl0d0VYell0YnlpUXxBQ3Jtc0trWGxseFptdEY5NENJZFRmRDltRExlTFhDUzNONDhxaVJMeDRjN1NIWl9xR1liQzdlR2VvX2Y1eVNtZV9TLWlvNmxBTW9lYTFzUUxISjZscHo5R0JJaDAtYVVRdW1DanB4VVRnN0lTeXlqalFVYzJMcw&amp;q=https%3A%2F%2Fteespring.com%2Fa2theshirt\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">https://teespring.com/a2theshirt</a>Follow the podcast hosts on social media: @a2theshow &nbsp;Hosts Ali Haejl @scoobz.mp4 alihaejl.com Ali Al Shammari @freshprinceofmishref &nbsp;Social Media Management @crooked.pearl &amp; @nad16er<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n</p>\n\n--- \n\nSend in a voice message: https://anchor.fm/a2theshow/message\nSupport this podcast: <a href=\"https://anchor.fm/a2theshow/support\" rel=\"payment\">https://anchor.fm/a2theshow/support</a>",
